Labels."SaveGiftsDesc".1 Note that there's no undo button and all saved selections are final.

KeyDescs."Loot" This key shows the items on the ground while it is pressed.
KeyDescs."Pri. Use" This key is used with the movement keys to carry out actions such as pick lock, disarm trap and open door.
KeyDescs."Sec. Use" This key is used with a hotkey to self cast spells, equip weapons in the offhand and to equip a ring on the offhand finger.
KeyDescs."Enter" This key is used to accept interface choices and to climb stairs up and down.
KeyDescs."Hotkey" Hotkeys can be used to quickly cast spells and use talents.
KeyDescs."Hotkey".1 You can bind a hotkey by pressing it while having the desired spell or talent selected in the spellbook window.
KeyDescs."Chat" This key shows the text field that can be used to send instant messages to other players (online only).
KeyDescs."Jump" This key can be used to jump in one of the four main directions (north, south, east, west).
KeyDescs."Swap" This key quickly swaps between the primary weapon set and the secondary weapon set.
KeyDescs."Equip" This key brings up the inventory window with an option to equip and unequip items.
KeyDescs."Sort" This key sorts the inventory.
KeyDescs."Travel" This key is used to quickly travel back to town after the current level has been cleared.
KeyDescs."Attack" This key brings up the attack cursor that can be used to attack enemies with ranged weapons.
KeyDescs."Search" This key is used to search the surroundings for traps and hidden features.
KeyDescs."Drop" This key shows the inventory window with an option to drop items.
KeyDescs."Throw" This key shows the inventory window with an option to throw items.
KeyDescs."Focus" This key brings up the focus cursor that can be used to order allies to focus on the chosen target.
KeyDescs."Cast" This key shows the spellbook that can be used to use talents and cast known spells.
KeyDescs."Look" This key brings up the look cursor that can be used to take a closer look at a target within range.
KeyDescs."Move N" This key moves the player or cursor up.
KeyDescs."Move S" This key moves the player or cursor down.
KeyDescs."Move E" This key moves the player or cursor right.
KeyDescs."Move W" This key moves the player or cursor left.
KeyDescs."Move NE" This key moves the player or cursor up and right.
KeyDescs."Move SE" This key moves the player or cursor down and right.
KeyDescs."Move NW" This key moves the player or cursor up and left.
KeyDescs."Move SW" This key moves the player or cursor down and left.
KeyDescs."Rest" This key is used to rest for one turn.
KeyDescs."Rest".1 Note that Keypad 5 requires that Num Lock is on and the 5 is a dead key otherwise (game engine feature).

Tooltips."ZAWACHI_DESC".2 - Six of a kind: 10x - 50x&#10;- Five of a kind: 5x&#10;- Four of a kind: 2x&#10;- Straight: 1x - 5x
Tooltips."ZAWACHI_DESC".3 Remaining re-rolls improve win multipliers by 10-20-40 or 1-2-4.

GUIDesc."PLAYER_STASH" This is your personal stash provided by Leo Noerde.
GUIDesc."PLAYER_STASH".1 Apparently he was so touched by your heroic deeds that he gave you access to some stash boxes in a secure room.
GUIDesc."MARKET_SQUARE" You have entered the Market Quarter and here you can trade items with various merchants.
GUIDesc."MARKET_SQUARE".1 Note that once the merchants' inventories  are filled with junk, you can reset them by resting in the inn.
GUIDesc."LEOS_WORKSHOP" You have entered Leo's Workshop and here you can have items crafted in exchange for materials and a few gold coins.
GUIDesc."LEOS_WORKSHOP".1 If you have crafting materials, schematics or gold, you can store them here to free up some inventory space.
GUIDesc."LEOS_WORKSHOP".2 Note that only stored materials can be used for crafting (drop an item to store it).
GUIDesc."ARTISAN_GUILD" You have entered the Artisans' Guild and here you can have your items repaired.
GUIDesc."ARTISAN_GUILD".1 If you have unique items, you can donate them to the guild with a drag and drop.
GUIDesc."ARTISAN_GUILD".2 If you have unidentified charms, you can identify them for free by attempting to donate them to the guild.
GUIDesc."ARTISAN_GUILD".3 Note that if you ever need to return some quest item then this is the place to do so.
GUIDesc."DIVINER_GUILD" You have entered the Diviners' Guild and here you can have your items identified.
GUIDesc."ENCHANT_GUILD" You have entered the Enchanters' Guild and here you can have your items enchanted.
GUIDesc."ENCHANT_GUILD".1 Items can usually have one enchant on them and blessed items can have two enchants.
GUIDesc."ENCHANT_GUILD".2 When you enchant an item you are given an option to choose from three possible outcomes.
GUIDesc."ENCHANT_GUILD".3 You can also cancel the selection in which case nothing changes, but you will not get your gold back.
GUIDesc."ENCHANT_GUILD".4 Note that some items, such as thrown weapons, do not give you a choice because they have their own rules for enchanting.
GUIDesc."NIBAR_SHRINE" You have entered the Shrine of Nibar and here you can remove curses and magical effects for a minor donation.
GUIDesc."FUBAR_SHRINE" You have entered the Shrine of Fubar and here you can remove poison and disease effects for a minor donation.
GUIDesc."FROSTMOURN_INN" You have entered the Frostmourn Inn where you can feast and rest while time passes by.
GUIDesc."FROSTMOURN_INN".1 If you choose to stay in the inn you will be fully healed and your hunger and thirst will be satiated.
GUIDesc."FROSTMOURN_INN".2 Another thing that happens is that the merchants in the Market Quarter will have their stocks reset.
GUIDesc."FROSTMOURN_INN".3 Finally, you will hear about a new dungeon nearby, which allows you to reset your current dungeon.
GUIDesc."FROSTMOURN_INN".4 Note that this also increases your chance of finding a random encounter when you do clear a dungeon.
GUIDesc."RESET_DUNGEON" Whether you have explored the current dungeon or spent some time feasting and resting, it matters not.
GUIDesc."RESET_DUNGEON".1 You are now ready to face new challenges just as soon as you want.
GUIDesc."RESET_DUNGEON".2 Be warned, however, that you should make sure you are fully prepared for anything that might show up...

TalentDescs."Aimed Shot" Ranged attack that causes D3 extra damage instead of 1 for each point of agility bonus modifier.
TalentDescs."Multi Shot" Ranged attack that hits up to agility bonus modifier number of extra targets.
TalentDescs."Quick Shot" Ranged attack that allows the creature to move before taking the shot.
TalentDescs."Steady Shot" Ranged attack that allows the creature to re-roll a failed to-hit check and doubles damage if used while hidden.
TalentDescs."Blade Flurry" Melee attack that gains up to one extra attack per weapon (at +1 and +3 AGI). Blade Flurry requires either two small
TalentDescs."Blade Flurry".1 weapons or a medium weapon that is used two-handedly.
TalentDescs."Deadly Throw" Thrown weapon attack that causes D3 extra damage instead of 1 for each point of strength or agility bonus modifier,
TalentDescs."Deadly Throw".1 whichever is higher (modifier also applies to to-hit checks).
TalentDescs."Heroic Charge" Allows the creature to move up to two spaces and attack a target at the end of the move.
TalentDescs."Heroic Charge".1 Also adds +1 damage modifier for the attack.
TalentDescs."Crushing Blow" Melee attack that causes D3 extra damage instead of 1 for each point of strength bonus modifier.
TalentDescs."Crushing Blow".1 Requires a medium or large weapon.
TalentDescs."Killing Blow" Melee attack that can instantly kill the target creature on hit (if the attack hits and the to-hit roll is a pair).
TalentDescs."Killing Blow".1 Requires a medium or large weapon.
TalentDescs."Sweeping Blow" Melee attack that hits the target creature and up to +STR adjacent targets. Requires a medium or large weapon and
TalentDescs."Sweeping Blow".1 grants +1 min block and +1 max parry modifier with large weapons.
TalentDescs."Shield Bash" Shield attack that can knock back and stun the target for D3 turns. This attack cannot be blocked, dodged, or
TalentDescs."Shield Bash".1 parried and causes the creature's deflect modifier to equal block modifier.
TalentDescs."Silent Move" Move action that hides the creature in plain sight. Melee attacks made while hidden and using Silent Move cause
TalentDescs."Silent Move".1 double damage and cannot be blocked, dodged or parried.
TalentDescs."Literacy: Common" Allows the creature to read and write Common, cast spells scribed on scrolls and zap with wands.
TalentDescs."Literacy: Celestial" Allows the creature to learn Celestial spells from magical tomes. Celestial spells always use Max Cast Modifier of 2
TalentDescs."Literacy: Celestial".1 or more regardless of armour.
TalentDescs."Literacy: Draconic" Allows the creature to learn Draconic spells from magical tomes.
TalentDescs."Literacy: Infernal" Allows the creature to learn Infernal spells from magical tomes.
TalentDescs."Focused Cast" Allows the creature to cast spells at any space within line of sight. Direct damage and healing spells receive extra
TalentDescs."Focused Cast".1 damage or healing depending on the relevant bonus modifier.
TalentDescs."Silent Cast" Allows the creature to cast spells while silenced and halves spell to-hit range modifier rounding down.
TalentDescs."Silent Cast".1 Silent Cast also teaches Clearcasting.
TalentDescs."Dark Vision" Increases light radius by 1 and halves ranged attack to-hit range modifier rounding down.
TalentDescs."Dual Wield" Offhand attacks no longer receive penalties to hit and damage and parry modifier equals to agility bonus modifier
TalentDescs."Dual Wield".1 instead of one half of it.
TalentDescs."Keen Eye" Allows the creature to re-roll failed search checks, increases search radius by 1 and grants a free action that
TalentDescs."Keen Eye".1 searches the surroundings when taking a move or rest action.
TalentDescs."Sixth Sense" Allows the creature to re-roll failed reflex checks and shows a warning before picking up or equipping an
TalentDescs."Sixth Sense".1 unidentified cursed item.
TalentDescs."Strong Will" Allows the creature to re-roll failed mental checks and halves the duration of charm, envy, fear, frenzy, greed, lust
TalentDescs."Strong Will".1 and reckless effects, rounding down.
TalentDescs."Trap Master" Allows the creature to see hidden bear traps and step on them without triggering the effects and allows the
TalentDescs."Trap Master".1 creature to disassemble bear traps into trap kits for later use.
TalentDescs."Shapeshift: Wolf" Shapeshifts the creature into a wolf and replaces all talents with Heroic Charge, Silent Move, Sixth Sense and
TalentDescs."Shapeshift: Wolf".1 Keen Eye (based on level).
TalentDescs."Shapeshift: Bear" Shapeshifts the creature into a bear and replaces all talents with Heroic Charge, Crushing Blow, Strong Will and
TalentDescs."Shapeshift: Bear".1 Keen Eye (based on level).
TalentDescs."Bestial Wrath" Increases physical damage by D3 while shapeshifted. This talent is also improved by the following heritages:
TalentDescs."Bestial Wrath".1 Bestial Vigour, Leader of the Pack.
TalentDescs."Slow and Steady" Ranged attacks made with slow weapons count as using both the Aimed Shot and Steady Shot talents at the same
TalentDescs."Slow and Steady".1 time and they use either strength or agility bonus modifier, whichever is higher.

TalentDescs."Shapeshift: Dingbat".1 Keen Eye (based on level).
TalentDescs."Summon Plague Bat" Special ability that allows the creature to summon a plague bat while in dingbat form.

TalentDescs."Sign Language".1 by randomly searching.

TalentDescs."Shapeshift: Demonrat".1 Blade Flurry (based on level).

TalentDescs."Daunting Charge" Expertise (Heroic Charge, Strong Will): Target must pass a mental check or become afraid for D3 turns.
TalentDescs."Mark Prey" Applies a Hunter's Mark on the target for 12 turns that increases ranged damage taken by 50% among other things.
TalentDescs."Sniper Shot" Expertise (Aimed Shot, Steady Shot): Ranged attack that counts as Aimed Shot and Steady Shot.
TalentDescs."Trap Vision" Expertise (Dark Vision, Trap Master): Trap Master also shows hidden pits.

TalentDescs."Takedown" Unarmed attack that uses up all of your remaining energy in an attempt to wrestle down and incapacitate a target.
TalentDescs."Takedown".1 More effective when used while hidden.

TalentDescs."Keen Senses".1 them.
TalentDescs."Wicked Throw" Expertise (Dark Vision, Deadly Throw): Thrown attacks gain +3 critical hit modifier, up to a maximum of +8.

SpellDescs."Cure Disease" Attempts to remove one disease effect from the target creature.
SpellDescs."Cure Poison" Attempts to remove one poison effect from the target creature.
SpellDescs."Dispel Magic" Attempts to remove one magical effect from the target creature, location or an item in the caster's inventory.
SpellDescs."Divine Grace" Increases agility and charisma and physical, poison and disease resistances.
SpellDescs."Divine Might" Increases strength and stamina and fire, frost and shock resistances.
SpellDescs."Divine Reach" Allows you to cast spells at any target within line of sight or halves the spell to-hit range modifier.
SpellDescs."Healing Touch" Heals the target creature and attempts to restore one point of ability damage.
SpellDescs."Healing Wave" Heals the target creature and all adjacent creatures.
SpellDescs."Renewing Touch" Places a heal over time effect on the target creature.
SpellDescs."Turn Undead" Causes magic damage or instantly kills the target undead creature.
SpellDescs."Amplify Magic" Places a magical effect on you that amplifies the damage of orb spells.
SpellDescs."Electric Orb" Causes shock damage to the target creature and has a chance of paralysing the target.
SpellDescs."Enlarge Orb" Places a magical effect on you that enlarges the next orb spell cast while the effect lasts.
SpellDescs."Flaming Orb" Causes fire damage to the target creature and has a chance of setting the target on fire.
SpellDescs."Frozen Orb" Causes frost damage to the target creature and has a chance of slowing the target.
SpellDescs."Illumination" Places a magical effect on all creatures within line of sight that increases light and search radius.
SpellDescs."Mage Armour" Places a magical effect on you that increases all resistances (the effect is removed if your equipment changes).
SpellDescs."Mirror Image" Creates a duplicate of the caster that can distract enemies.
SpellDescs."Remove Curse" Attempts to remove one curse effect from the target creature, location or an item in the caster's inventory.
SpellDescs."Telekinesis" Allows the caster to magically use remote objects such as doors, chests, levers and so on.
SpellDescs."Banish Daemon" Causes magic damage or instantly kills the target daemon.
SpellDescs."Bestow Curse" Attempts to place a random curse effect on the target creature or Curse of Agony if the check fails.
SpellDescs."Capture Soul" Places a magical effect on the target creature that turns its soul to a soul gem upon death.
SpellDescs."Demonic Visage" Places a magical effect on you that forces attackers to take a fear check.
SpellDescs."Enslave Daemon" Attempts to temporarily charm a daemon and make it your friend.
SpellDescs."Plane Shift" Attempts to teleport the caster to another location within line of sight.
SpellDescs."Release Soul" Releases a soul from a random soul gem on the target creature or an item in the caster's inventory.
SpellDescs."Summon Daemon" Attempts to summon a daemon and then attempts to enslave it.
SpellDescs."Venomous Orb" Causes poison damage to the target creature and has a chance of applying a random poison effect.
SpellDescs."Virulent Orb" Causes disease damage to the target creature and has a chance of applying a random disease effect.
SpellDescs."Divine Shield" Creates a shield around the caster that absorbs damage until it breaks.
SpellDescs."Conjure Daemon" Summons a lesser daemon at the target location and enslaves it.
SpellDescs."Identify Item" Identifies the targeted item in the caster's inventory.
SpellDescs."Enchant Item" Enchants the targeted item in the caster's inventory with a random enchant.
SpellDescs."Elemental Orb" Causes fire, frost and shock damage to the target and all adjacent creatures.
SpellDescs."Clone Creature" Creates a clone of the target creature that aids the caster for awhile.
SpellDescs."Animate Dead" Permanently turns a dead human into an undead familiar.
SpellDescs."Transmute Item" Transmutes the targeted item in the caster's inventory into gold coins.
SpellDescs."Alter Terrain" Increases or decreases the height of terrain on even or odd turns respectively.
SpellDescs."Arcane Missile" Causes magic damage or instantly kills the target creature.
SpellDescs."Big Bear Slap" Attempts to disarm, knock back and stun the target creature.
SpellDescs."Command Beast" Attempts to control the target beast and make it your friend.
SpellDescs."Cure Bleeding" Attempts to remove a bleeding wound from the target creature.
SpellDescs."Expose Roots" Spawns a treeman from the target mushroom patch.
SpellDescs."Fairy Flight" Places a magical effect on you that makes you levitate.
SpellDescs."Insect Swarm" Attempts to overcome the target creature with various effects.
SpellDescs."Raptor Strike" Tears open a wound and causes the target to bleed.
SpellDescs."Shroom Grenade" Throws a random blood cap from the caster's inventory and explodes it on impact.
SpellDescs."Soothe Beast" Attempts to soothe the target beast and make it neutral towards you.
SpellDescs."Spirit Wolves" Summons a pack of ethereal spirit wolves at the target location.
SpellDescs."Abyssal Grasp" Summons an abyssal claw at the target location.
SpellDescs."Army of the Dead" Consumes all soul gems in your inventory to spawn an army of the dead.
SpellDescs."Corrupting Cloud" Creates a corrupting cloud at the target location hitting everyone inside.
SpellDescs."Dancing Weapons" Summons dancing weapons at the target location.
SpellDescs."Grounding Orb" Causes magic damage based on the remaining energy and maximum mana shield of the target creature.
SpellDescs."Mass Dismissal" Attempts to unsummon all summoned creatures within line of sight.
SpellDescs."Repelling Smite" Attempts to knock back and stun all adjacent creatures.
SpellDescs."Ritual Sacrifice" Attempts to sacrifice a creature at the center of the nearest sacrificial circle.
SpellDescs."Sacrificial Circle" Conjures a 3x3 sacrificial circle at the target location.
SpellDescs."Spectral Gateway" Teleports you to the nearest sacrificial circle or a random location if none exists.

TutorialDescs."Introduction 1".1 first time you're playing this game...

TutorialDescs."Introduction 2".1 over the Internet...
TutorialDescs."Move Buttons" Allrighty then. You can move onto any of the eight adjacent tiles by using the keypad or by clicking in the desired
TutorialDescs."Move Buttons".1 direction...
TutorialDescs."Basic Attack" Now that looks like a nasty creature. If you want, you can attack it by moving towards it...
TutorialDescs."Use Button" You can use adjacent map objects or items by holding down the Ctrl-key and pressing the relevant movement key
TutorialDescs."Use Button".1 or by right-clicking in the desired direction...
TutorialDescs."Loot Button" You can view the loot under your feet by holding down the Loot-key (Default: Alt) or by clicking the right side of the
TutorialDescs."Loot Button".1 screen...
TutorialDescs."Rest Button" Whenever you're fatigued or wounded, you can rest and gain energy or health with the Rest-button (Default: Keypad5)
TutorialDescs."Rest Button".1 or by clicking yourself...
TutorialDescs."Satiated Rest" Note, however, that in order to gain health, you must have both hunger and thirst satiated (see the bottom right
TutorialDescs."Satiated Rest".1 corner)...
TutorialDescs."Equip Button" You can equip and use items in the inventory after bringing it up with the Equip-button (Default: E) or by clicking on
TutorialDescs."Equip Button".1 the right side of the screen...
TutorialDescs."Offhand Equip" While the inventory is shown, you can equip and use items with the Enter-key. If you also hold down the Shift-key
TutorialDescs."Offhand Equip".1 you can equip an item in the offhand...
TutorialDescs."Mouse Equip" Alternatively, you can click an item to use or equip it or you can drag and drop the item in the chosen slot (or out of
TutorialDescs."Mouse Equip".1 the inventory)...
TutorialDescs."Drop Button" You can drop items from the inventory after bringing it up with the Drop-button (Default: D) or you can drag and
TutorialDescs."Drop Button".1 drop them using a mouse...
TutorialDescs."Throw Button" You can throw items from the inventory after bringing it up with the Throw-button (Default: F) or you can right-click
TutorialDescs."Throw Button".1 throw them with a mouse...
TutorialDescs."Attack Button" Excellent! I see you have found yourself a ranged weapon. You can make ranged attacks with the Attack-button
TutorialDescs."Attack Button".1 (Default: A)...
TutorialDescs."Rearm Button" Your weapon needs to be rearmed before it can be used again. This is done automatically if you rest while having
TutorialDescs."Rearm Button".1 such a weapon equipped...
TutorialDescs."Use Entrances" You can use stairs and ladders by pressing the Enter-key or by right-clicking yourself...
TutorialDescs."Talent Gain 1" Oh look, you have earned your first talent point. You can spend it by visiting a trainer or by using one of the trainer
TutorialDescs."Talent Gain 1".1 tiles...
TutorialDescs."Talent Gain 2" Note, however, that you can learn a maximum of six talents and there's no money back guarantee, so choose them
TutorialDescs."Talent Gain 2".1 wisely...
TutorialDescs."Use Talents" Great choice! You can use the talent you just learned through the spellbook by pressing the Cast-button (Default: C)...
TutorialDescs."Cast Spells" Way to go you little Wizard! You can cast the spell you just learned through the spellbook by pressing the Cast-button
TutorialDescs."Cast Spells".1 (Default: C)...
TutorialDescs."Bind Hotkeys" You can bind and unbind spells and active talents on hotkeys by selecting one and pressing a Hotkey-button
TutorialDescs."Bind Hotkeys".1 (Default: 1,2,3,4,5,6,7)...
TutorialDescs."Order Button" Oh look, you have gained a friend. You can order friends to follow you, move to a location or attack a target with the
TutorialDescs."Order Button".1 Focus-key (Default: X)...
TutorialDescs."Travel Button" Great job, you've cleared the dungeon. Now you can quickly travel back to town with the Travel-button (Default: T)...
TutorialDescs."Search Button" Ouch, that's gotta hurt. I don't want to rub it in but you could've found the trap with the Search-button (Default: S)...

MobileTutorials."Throw Button".1 on an item until you hear a click sound)...

ChallengeDescs."Enchanting Patron" This challenge can be completed by magically blessing an item at the Enchanters' Guild.
ChallengeDescs."PartialChallenge" This is a part of the %s challenge.
ChallengeDescs."Hand Collector" This challenge can be completed by selling 12 of each hand to the guild vendor in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Egg Collector" This challenge can be completed by selling 12 spider eggs to the guild vendor in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Eye Collector" This challenge can be completed by selling 12 floater eyes to the guild vendor in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Slug Collector" This challenge can be completed by selling 12 slug chitins to the guild vendor in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Worm Collector" This challenge can be completed by selling 12 brain worms to the guild vendor in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Coin Collector" This challenge can be completed by selling 12 dragon coins to the guild vendor in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Trophy Collector" This challenge can be completed by completing all of the Expertise DLC collector challenges above.
ChallengeDescs."One Shot One Kill" This challenge can be completed by killing an uninjured encounter boss with a single sniper shot.
ChallengeDescs."One Shot One Kill".1 Encounter bosses have unique names and they can show up when you clear a dungeon.
ChallengeDescs."One Shot One Kill".2 You must be level 20 and instant kill effects do not count.
ChallengeDescs."Inquiring Mind" This challenge can be completed by asking the magic mirror all three questions in one game.
ChallengeDescs."Guild jobs completed:" Guild jobs completed:
ChallengeDescs."GuildJobsOnly" Only guild specific trial jobs and jobs started at the guild hall count for this challenge.
ChallengeDescs."Master Fighter" This challenge can be completed by finishing 9 or more Fighters' Guild jobs in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Master Hunter" This challenge can be completed by finishing 9 or more Hunters' Guild jobs in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Master Wizard" This challenge can be completed by finishing 9 or more Wizards' Guild jobs in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Master Thief" This challenge can be completed by finishing 9 or more Thieves' Guild jobs in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Guild Master" This challenge can be completed by reaching max rank in all 4 guilds in a single game.
ChallengeDescs."Guild Master".1 The only way to leave a guild amicably is to give a Core of Regret to the guild vendor.
ChallengeDescs."Guild Master".2 You may have to complete a Sinister Ritual in order to obtain the third core (sorry Woof).

RuleDescs."No Retreat" Leaving from a job before the music has stopped is dishonorable.
RuleDescs."No Wastage" Leaving free range meat on the ground is considered wasteful.
RuleDescs."No Witchery" Ailments, daemons and necromancy makes the public feel nervous.
RuleDescs."No Murders" Killing a human draws too much unwanted attention to the guild.
RuleDescs."Kill Them" Kill all enemies and clear the dungeon.
RuleDescs."Chop Them" Kill all enemies with a chopping weapon.
RuleDescs."Crush Them" Kill all enemies with a crushing weapon.
RuleDescs."Flail Them" Kill all enemies with a flailing weapon.
RuleDescs."Pierce Them" Kill all enemies with a piercing weapon.
RuleDescs."Slash Them" Kill all enemies with a slashing weapon.
RuleDescs."Beat Them" Kill all enemies with unarmed attacks.
RuleDescs."Strike Them" Kill all enemies with a melee weapon.
RuleDescs."Shoot Them" Kill all enemies with a ranged weapon.
RuleDescs."Pelt Them" Kill all enemies with a thrown weapon.
RuleDescs."Burn Them" Kill all enemies with fire damage.
RuleDescs."Freeze Them" Kill all enemies with frost damage.
RuleDescs."Shock Them" Kill all enemies with shock damage.
RuleDescs."Poison Them" Kill all enemies with poison damage.
RuleDescs."Infect Them" Kill all enemies with disease damage.
RuleDescs."Curse Them" Kill all enemies with magic damage.
RuleDescs."Taunt Them" Kill all enemies while they are demoralized.
RuleDescs."Mark Them" Kill all enemies while they are marked.
RuleDescs."Snare Them" Kill all enemies while they are snared.
RuleDescs."Escort Job" Bring the escortee to stairs leading down.
RuleDescs."Rescue Job" Find and bring the rescuee over to the exit.
RuleDescs."Clean Job" Do not kill anyone or break anything.
RuleDescs."Inside Job" Close all gates before leaving the dungeon.
RuleDescs."Mundane Job" Do not cast spells or use magic of any kind.
RuleDescs."Silent Job" Do not set off an alarm or allow a guard to do so.
RuleDescs."Hands Off" Do not loot from or break any storage containers (except quest items and clues).
RuleDescs."Fetch Item" Loot a specified quest item and get to the exit.
RuleDescs."Plant Item" Drop a quest item at a specified location and get to the exit.
RuleDescs."Grand Heist" Loot all specified quest items and get to the exit.
RuleDescs."Sightseeing" Leave the dungeon before escape timer hits 0 or you will be expelled from the guild.

TcgInfoTexts."Select an effect in your hand to exhaust." Select an effect in your hand to exhaust.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 1" Agony - Damage over time that deals 3, 5, 6+ damage at the end of the turn.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 2" Burn - Damage over time that deals 3, 5, 6+ damage at the end of the turn.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 3" Wound - Damage over time that deals 3, 5, 6+ damage at the end of the turn.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 4" Charm - Miss your normal action and gain 1 evasion (take a dodge action instead).
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 5" Daze - Miss your normal action (take a sleep action instead).
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 6" Morph - Miss your normal action (take an attack action instead).
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 7" Decoy - The next attack made against you is ignored.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 8" Evasion - Reduces the damage of the next attack by 50%.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 9" Hidden - Reduces the damage of the next attack by 100%.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 10" Resist - Prevents the next DoT or CC (NPC) or exhausts the next harmful card that is drawn.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 11" Spikes - Deals 3, 5, 6+ damage to the attacker. If the attacker dies you take no damage.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 12" Focus - Spells gain +3 damage for each point of focus.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 13" Strength - Attacks gain +3 damage for each point of strength.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 14" Power Up - Attacks and spells do double damage for each power up.
TcgInfoTexts."Effect 15" Soul Gem - Some spells require soul gems before they can be cast.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 1" Miss next action.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 2" Do something special (power up or summon).
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 3" Do something unknown (buff, defend or whatever).
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 4" Perform basic attack.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 5" Perform basic attack and apply curse if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 6" Perform basic attack and apply poison if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 7" Perform basic attack and apply disease if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 8" Perform basic attack and apply burn if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 9" Perform basic attack and apply chill if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 10" Perform basic attack and apply fear if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 11" Perform basic attack and apply shock if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 12" Perform basic attack and apply stun if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 13" Perform basic attack and apply wound if damage is caused.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 14" Perform basic attack and break armour and evasion.
TcgInfoTexts."Intent 15" Perform double attack.
